New pure `src/lib/composition.ts` — Layer-2 (per-type default) + Layer-3 (per-record) shapes (`Composition`/`RecordWidget`, reusing the dashboard grid cell), tolerant `parseComposition`, `reconcileComposition` (drop removed widgets), `resolveComposition` overlay (record → type → generated, the `resolveLayout` pattern), the default **Project** composition (PRD §8 header strip + center + thin Tasks rail) with Digest-on, and gear helpers (`addableWidgets`/`isWidgetEnabled`); disable = `hidden:true` (hide-not-delete). `ViewFilter` gains **`relatedHome`** + **`relatedRole`** — a containment refinement of `relatedTo` (directional child→parent home edge) so a record-scoped Tasks/Notes widget surfaces what LIVES on the record, not everything related; additive, existing `relatedTo` behavior unchanged when unset. The `resolveRecordWidgets` rendering fan-out is deferred to PJ4 (where the canvas consumes it).
**Why / alternatives:** *Catalog as code, not a DB table* — mirrors the module registry; the catalog is code-owned and the gear reads it. *Availability derived, not curated* — the PRD's Layer 1; the explicit `SATISFIABLE` set is the one place a future type-capability gate would live. *Composition parse tolerant + overlay* — matches `canvas-layout.ts`/`dashboards.ts` so a malformed blob degrades to the default, never errors. *relatedHome directional* — "what lives here" is the child→parent home edge, distinct from the direction-blind `relatedTo`.
**Verification:** `scripts/verify-widget-catalog.mts` 22/22 on Neon (availability is whole-catalog for any type incl. an unknown one; record-only vs both-scope widgets; default composition incl. §8 + Digest; tolerant parse/dedupe/reconcile/overlay precedence; live home-scoped + role-scoped queries return only contained children). `verify-views`/`verify-dashboards`/`verify-project`/`verify-list-lenses`/`verify-embedded-views` regress green; tsc/eslint/`next build` clean. No migration.
**Affects:** new `src/lib/widgets.ts` + `src/lib/composition.ts`, `src/lib/views.ts` (`ViewFilter` + `viewWhere` + parse), `scripts/verify-widget-catalog.mts`.

### PJ4 (2026-06-29) — widget canvas shell + gear (project page is widget-composed)
**Decision:** A `widget-home` capability (registered in `coreModule`, canvasId `widgets`) routes a type's records through the new `WidgetCanvas`; `module-wiring.tsx` maps `widgets` → `WidgetCanvas`; migration 0036 + `seed.mjs` set the `project` type's `capability='widget-home'` (so `canvasIdForType` resolves it via the existing ADR-051 SPIKE capability seam — any type adopts it in PJ10, zero new routing). New server `src/lib/record-widgets.ts` `resolveRecordWidgets(ownerId, record, composition)` — DashboardView's per-widget fan-out generalized to record scope: each collection/relation widget binds `relatedTo = record.id` (home-scoped + role-scoped for contained collections via PJ3's `relatedHome`/`relatedRole`; people are direction-blind), derived/property widgets read the base + activity log; Progress is indeterminate at zero tasks (never 0%). `WidgetCanvas` (server) resolves the composition (record → type → generated §8 default), fans out, renders the title (`ItemEditor`) + each widget in its saved lg grid position; bodies = Overview (editable body), Status pill, home-scoped collection lists, Next Action, Progress bar, Recent Activity. `WidgetGear` (client) is the "Customize" surface — section 1 (which-widgets: enable/disable = hide-not-delete, the first edit lazily materializes the full resolved composition onto `items.composition`; reset = composition null). `types.defaultWidgets` exposed raw on `TypeDefinition`.
**Why / alternatives:** *Capability seam over adding project to coreModule.types* — keeps project a normal DB type, opt-in, and generalizes to PJ10. *Render in saved positions (no RGL drag yet)* — defer-by-hiding: the §8 layout reads right via a 12-col grid; interactive drag-arrange is a follow-up, not v1-blocking. *Tasks/Notes read-only here* — editable bodies are PJ5; PJ4 is the shell.
**Verification:** `scripts/verify-widget-canvas.mts` 17/17 on Neon (project routes to widgets; born with the §8 defaults; fan-out is home-scoped — Tasks widget shows the contained task, not an unrelated one; disable hides + keeps the item + re-enable restores; reset clears; Next Action + Recent Activity read base/log). `verify-types`/`verify-canvas-seam`/`verify-bespoke-capability`/`verify-project` regress green; fixed a stale `verify-module-registry` assertion (task has its own canvas since ADR-108). tsc/eslint/`next build` clean. Migration 0036 applied. In-browser eyeball deferred.
**Affects:** `src/lib/modules.ts` (capability), `src/lib/module-wiring.tsx` (canvas map), `src/lib/types.ts` (defaultWidgets), `drizzle/0036_project_widget_home.sql` + journal, `scripts/seed.mjs`, new `src/lib/record-widgets.ts` + `src/components/canvas/WidgetCanvas.tsx` + `WidgetGear.tsx`, `scripts/verify-widget-canvas.mts`.

### PJ5 (2026-06-29) — editable collection widgets + milestone type
**Decision:** New `milestone` system type (migration 0037 + seed): a polymorphic collection item with NO done-state — date = `due_date`, upcoming/passed derived from the clock, `status_mode='none'`, hidden + out of quick capture; attaches to ANY type via a home edge. Next Action auto-advance (`items.ts` done-block + `advanceNextActionIfPinned`): completing the home parent's pinned task advances `next_action_task_id` to the next open contained task (ordered by creation) else clears it — a direct owner-scoped write (no `updateItem` recursion). `POST /api/records/[id]/contain` — the one write path behind the editable widgets (create + home-contain; tasks role "project", else "contains"). Three client widget bodies: `TasksWidget` (add / check-off / pin-as-Next-Action), `NotesWidget` (scratch capture bar → untitled note on blur/Enter, then clears — PRD §6 one-surface-two-states), `MilestonesWidget` (add label+date, derived passed/upcoming badge), wired into `WidgetCanvas`.
**Verification:** `scripts/verify-record-widgets.mts` 11/11 on Neon (milestone type props; polymorphic attach to a non-project parent; no done-state; pin auto-advance incl. a non-pinned completion leaving the pin alone; milestone fan-out). `verify-items`/`verify-recurrence`/`verify-record-base`/`verify-widget-canvas`/`verify-activity-log` regress green; tsc/eslint/`next build` clean. Migration 0037. In-browser eyeball deferred.
**Affects:** `drizzle/0037_milestone_type.sql` + journal, `scripts/seed.mjs`, `src/lib/items.ts` (auto-advance), new `src/app/api/records/[id]/contain/route.ts` + `src/components/canvas/widgets/{Tasks,Notes,Milestones}Widget.tsx`, `src/components/canvas/WidgetCanvas.tsx`.

### PJ6 (2026-06-29) — derived lenses → the usable project page
**Decision:** Progress is hierarchical (PRD §6): a leaf task is 0/1, a parent's fraction is the average of its task-children's fractions (recursive over the `parent_id` subtree via `listSubtree`), and the bar is the average of the top-level contained tasks' fractions; `flat` weighting stays done/total. Zero tasks → indeterminate (null, never 0%); 100% suggests Done but the project is never auto-forced. Deep-compute is capped (200 top-level tasks) so a large forest can't fan out unbounded. Next Action + Recent Activity bodies were wired in PJ4. **This reaches the PRD "shippable project page" milestone (end of phase 2): a project is born with default widgets, arrangeable via the gear, Tasks/Notes editable, milestones + derived lenses live.**
**Verification:** `scripts/verify-derived-widgets.mts` 10/10 on Neon (indeterminate-at-zero; hierarchical 0.5 vs flat 0 on a half-done subtree; 3-level recursion; 100% not auto-forced; Next Action title + activity lines). `verify-widget-canvas`/`verify-record-widgets`/`verify-subtasks` regress green; tsc/eslint/`next build` clean. No migration.
**Affects:** `src/lib/record-widgets.ts` (hierarchical progress + `nodeFraction`/`rootFraction`), `scripts/verify-derived-widgets.mts`.

### PJ7 (2026-06-29) — Digest / check-ins behavior (push-first)
**Decision:** The Digest is a behavior, not a widget (PRD §7) — it pings about projects gone quiet (staleness) or with a milestone coming up; deterministic, no model (Principle 3). Pure `src/lib/digest/compose.ts`: digestStatus (staleness wins over upcoming; no-activity-ever = dont nag; a recent review resets the clock), composeDigest (the PRD payload from Recent Activity + Milestones + Next Action), daysUntil. `src/lib/digest/notify.ts` runDigestNotify selects project items whose resolved composition has behaviors.digest.enabled, computes staleness (derived lastActivityAt/lastReviewedAt) + upcoming contained milestones, composes, pushes via the existing sendToOwner/WebPushSender, dedups one ping per staleness window (a properties.notify.digestNotifiedAt stamp, the prepNotifiedAt pattern). /api/machine/notify-digest cron + a daily vercel.json entry. activity.ts gains lastActivityAt. The review-resets-clock loop is already first-class (PJ1 checkin_reviewed → derived last_reviewed_at).
**Why / alternatives:** Push-first, email deferred — push is built + reachable; outbound email is not built, so it is a flagged fast-follow behind a future MailSender seam (the compose/select logic is channel-agnostic; reverses the PRD §7 email-first guess). No new notifications table — origin/main already ships the notifications table (ADR-129/130); a duplicate on the stale local base would be throwaway, so PJ7 only pushes + stamps and reuses that table at integration (a known reconciliation). Staleness over a dumb timer — the activity log makes quiet the smart trigger.
**Verification:** scripts/verify-digest.mts 16/16 on Neon — pure status/payload/daysUntil + live (under a THROWAWAY owner so real projects are untouched): fresh-doesnt-ping, stale-pings, dedup, upcoming-milestone-pings, recent-review-resets. verify-activity-log/verify-push/verify-containment regress green; tsc/eslint/next build clean. In-browser (a real push landing) deferred.
**Affects:** new src/lib/digest/{compose,notify}.ts, src/lib/activity.ts (lastActivityAt), new src/app/api/machine/notify-digest/route.ts, vercel.json, scripts/verify-digest.mts.

### PJ8 (2026-06-29) — Overview weave (two-zone Head/Story)
**Decision:** The Overview is one markdown body in two zones (PRD §6): the Head (evergreen, overwritten) and the Story (accreting, a readable post-mortem). New `src/lib/overview/weave.ts`: splitHeadStory/appendToStory (a "## Story" section, the Head untouched), buildStorySkeleton (dated bullets from activity, oldest-first), gatherUnwoven (events since the last weave), weaveStory (append + version + emit overview_woven), proposeStoryUpdate. GET/POST `/api/records/[id]/weave` (propose the editable skeleton, accept the edited lines). updateItem auto-snapshots the body change so each weave is versioned; overview_woven advances the derived last_woven_at (activity.ts gains lastWovenAt). Principle 3 / ADR-087: deterministic parts in-app; the optional prose polish (skeleton → narrative) is a Claude-over-MCP step, NOT an in-app LLM call (no new dependency); pure-auto narration rejected.
**Verification:** scripts/verify-overview-weave.mts 14/14 on Neon (pure split/append/skeleton; live propose-gathers-only-post-weave, weave appends + keeps Head + advances clock + snapshots a revision). Regressions green; tsc/eslint/build clean. The in-widget editing UI is a follow-up.
**Affects:** new src/lib/overview/weave.ts, src/lib/activity.ts (lastWovenAt), new src/app/api/records/[id]/weave/route.ts, scripts/verify-overview-weave.mts.

### PJ9 (2026-06-29) — containment up (Pursuit + Related Records + roll-up)
**Decision:** Pursuit is a widget-composed Type one scope up (PRD §1) — contains Projects via home edges the same way a Project contains tasks; not special-cased (carries widget-home, is a tracked subject). pursuit type (migration 0038 + seed). Roll-up in record-widgets.ts: a record that contains projects shows Progress = average of its projects fractions (done = number complete, total = number of projects), Recent Activity = the union of its own + its projects logs (new activity.listActivityForSubjects), Next Action = the first contained project next step when the record has none. A plain project (contains tasks, not projects) is unaffected. Related Records honors the type-filter option + the home flag. isTrackedSubjectType now includes pursuit.
**Verification:** scripts/verify-pursuit-rollup.mts 10/10 on Neon (routing; containment; type-filtered Related Records; Progress avg; activity union; Next Action roll-up). Regressions green; tsc/eslint/build clean. Migration 0038.
**Affects:** drizzle/0038_pursuit_type.sql + journal, scripts/seed.mjs, src/lib/activity.ts, src/lib/composition.ts, src/lib/record-widgets.ts, scripts/verify-pursuit-rollup.mts.

### PJ10 (2026-06-29) — universal per-type homepages (verified)
**Decision:** The widget-composed homepage is a capability ANY type can adopt in Build, not Project-only (Tyler scope expansion). It fell out of the model: PJ4 registered widget-home as an attachable capability + Layer-1 availability is universal, so the existing ADR-051 capability seam already lets a user attach "Widget homepage" to any type → it routes to the widget canvas, inherits the whole catalog with zero widget authoring, and gets a generated default composition (an authored types.default_widgets wins when present). No new code.
**Verification:** scripts/verify-type-homepage.mts 6/6 on Neon (widget-home is attachable; an arbitrary type routes to widgets + inherits the full catalog + gets a default; an authored Layer-2 default is honored). The acceptance criterion "a new Type needs zero widget authoring" is met. Follow-up: a visual Build "Design homepage" editor for default_widgets.
**Affects:** scripts/verify-type-homepage.mts (verification only).

### PJ11 (2026-06-29) — Mindmap + Timeline widgets
**Decision:** Timeline (derived): a read-only overlay of the record Meetings + Milestones by date, shown together without merging their data (PRD §6) — fan-out queries contained events + milestones, the body renders a dated kind-tagged list. Mindmap (collection, cardinality one): surfaces the record contained mindmap(s) linking to the existing MindmapCanvas, via the generic collection path (the mindmap module is reused, not reimplemented). v2 node-promotion (graph node → task/note/milestone) is explicitly deferred.
**Verification:** scripts/verify-graph-widgets.mts 3/3 on Neon (timeline overlays + date-sorts a meeting + milestone; mindmap widget lists the contained mindmap). Regressions green; tsc/eslint/build clean.
**Affects:** src/lib/record-widgets.ts (timeline fan-out), src/components/canvas/WidgetCanvas.tsx (timeline body), scripts/verify-graph-widgets.mts.

### ADR-138 closeout (2026-06-29) — PJ1–PJ11 complete on local main; integration pending
**Status:** the full PJ series (PJ1–PJ11) is built, verified, and merged to LOCAL main. **Not yet integrated onto origin/main**, which diverged ~242 files at session start (Brandon's PRs up to #128). Integration work, agreed deferred with Tyler: (1) renumber migrations 0034–0038 (origin already holds 0034–0039); (2) reconcile conflicts in views.ts (origin +110), items.ts, schema.ts, modules/types, seed.mjs; (3) **rebind PJ7's Digest persistence to Brandon's existing `notifications` table (ADR-129/130)** rather than the push-only stub; (4) reconcile the PRD "archived" boolean with Brandon's in-flight `items.archived_at` axis (deferred in PJ2). Plus in-browser eyeball passes (deferred per slice — strong server-side verify + clean builds in the meantime).

## ADR-139: Live item tokens — `{{item.*}}` in the canonical body, resolved at render time
**Date:** 2026-07-02
**Status:** accepted (Brandon; **Tyler ack pending** — flagged in `COLLAB.md`). **CORE** — extends the canonical body format (the `{format, text}` contract): a markdown body may now carry *live tokens* that are derived from the item's current state, not literal text. First slice (LT1) of the plan in `explorations/live-item-tokens.md`.
**Context:** Brandon (2026-07-02) wants a body that pulls in the item's own facts and its relations so he never edits the same thing twice: a paper whose printed/exported body carries the due date from its property; a `[Title]`-style token echoing the item title; a note that lists its related people. The 2026-06-20 templates redesign (ADR-093) already covers the *apply-time* half (bake `{{today}}`/`{{ask:}}` once when a template stamps an item). What's new is the *render-time* half: tokens that stay in the stored markdown and re-resolve every time the body is rendered. That's a body-format extension, not a templates feature — templates inherit it for free because the apply resolver leaves unknown tokens intact, so a prototype's live tokens survive the clone.
**Decision:**
1. **Two resolution times, kept separate.** Apply-time vars (`template-vars.ts`, baked once) and live tokens (`item-tokens.ts`, resolved per render) are distinct namespaces and distinct code. A live token is always `{{item.*}}`, `{{parent.*}}`, `{{item.children}}`, or `{{item.related.<key>}}`; anything else (including apply-time vars) passes through the live resolver untouched. This is what makes the two layers compose on one body.
2. **Grammar (the contract).** Scalars `{{item.title|status|type|url|priority}}`; dates `{{item.due|scheduled|created|meeting}}` with `:iso/long/short/us/day` formats and `±Nd/w/m/y` arithmetic; `{{item.props.<key>}}` (a `YYYY-MM-DD` value gets date treatment, else plain text); lists `{{item.children}}` and `{{item.related.<roleOrType>}}` (keyed by BOTH edge role and target type) that render comma-joined inline or as a real `ul`/`ol` list **only when the token is alone on its line**; `{{parent.*}}` for subtask bodies; `\{{…}}` escapes. Full table in the exploration doc.
3. **Pure resolver + DB context, mirroring the templates split.** `src/lib/item-tokens.ts` is pure/client-safe (the caller passes `todayYmd` + a plain context), so it's node-testable and can back a client preview later. `src/lib/item-tokens-service.ts` (`buildItemTokenContext`) does ONE owner-scoped, **body-free** read of the item + parent + children (authoring order) + outgoing relations — never another item's body (the list-query rule).
4. **Related/children ride the mention pipeline.** A list token emits `[@Title](ledgr://item/<id>)`, the exact mention-link shape (`mention-markdown.ts`). Callers resolve tokens **before** collecting `@`-mentions, so token-emitted links land in the mentions map and render type-aware (glyph + link), and flatten to plain names on print/share like any mention.
5. **Render-only; the token is the source of truth.** Resolution never writes the DB. It runs in `markdownToHtml`'s callers: `/items/[id]/print` (Save Offline), `/share/[token]`, and `/api/render-markdown` (the live Preview, which gained an optional `itemId`). **FTS strips tokens** (`markdownToText`) rather than indexing a resolved value that would silently go stale.
6. **Back-compat + additive.** A body with no live tokens renders byte-identical; chordpro (non-markdown) bodies are not token-resolved in v1; no schema change, no migration.
**Alternatives considered:** (a) bake live values into the body on save (rejected — defeats the whole "edit once" point and goes stale on rename/re-date); (b) resolve inside `markdownToHtml` with the token context passed through (rejected — the mentions map is built by the caller and must see post-resolution text, so callers own the ordering); (c) `[Title]` square-bracket syntax (rejected — collides with markdown link labels).
**Verification:** `scripts/verify-item-tokens.mts` 58/58 (pure grammar: every token kind, date math/format, inline vs block lists, escaping, unknown/apply-time passthrough; + live Neon: context fields, children order, owner-scoping of the item and of related targets, and `resolveItemBodyTokens` rewriting title + body). `verify-body-contract`/`verify-body-modes` green; tsc/eslint/`next build` clean.
**Affects:** src/lib/item-tokens.ts (new), src/lib/item-tokens-service.ts (new), src/lib/markdown-render.ts (unchanged — callers orchestrate), src/app/items/[id]/print/route.ts, src/app/share/[token]/route.ts, src/app/api/render-markdown/route.ts, src/components/markdown-editor/MarkdownPreview.tsx + BodyEditor.tsx, scripts/verify-item-tokens.mts (new). Follow-ons (non-core): LT2 editor chips, TPL6 apply-time gaps, LT3 export/MCP parity — see `explorations/live-item-tokens.md`.
